This place was amazing at everything up until 2/28 when they re-opened the kitchen with a new Chef.Specifically the Curry. I tried POV for this first time yesterday and was so impressed by the quality and taste of all my food. I ordered the 5 Cheese pizza special on Fridays for $10, the Big Kahuna, and the Altadena salad. Everything was terrific and the pizza toppings were legit! They have out door seating with a fireplace.. the place is beautiful at night because they have everything lit up. They have quite the variety of toppings to choose from. The last time I went, I got the prisoners pizza which crust was stuffed with ricotta. Super friendly, I'd recommend guest to try this place if they get the chance!</review>

< review>
I'm a big fan of shabu shabu and this place is just OK. ($20- $17 for a large order) When you come in you choose the kind of broth you want, the meat you want and size.  Pretty standard. The amount and variety of veggies they offer leave alot to be desired. Cabbage, bok choy, 2 small pieces of carrot and 2 small broccoli florets... THATS IT?! No mushrooms? Which you normally get shiitake and enokitake. No nori or green onions for flavor.  You do get noodles and 2 pieces of tofu but again the serving is significantly smaller than in other places.
Overall shabu shabu is a fun experience so the visit was fine. The service wad really nice and the place is spotless and we'll kept. As far as flavor and quality you're better off going down the street to shabu shabu house (also on convoy) way more flavorful and better veggie servings and variety (also a bit cheaper)< /review>

It should be noted that a couple of the tables had a "reserved" plackard on them, but most empty tables did NOT. After pressing about the number of empty tables, the hostess said she would check, walked away and proceeded to ignore us.  A couple minutes later, a server came by and asked if we had a reservation (!?!?).  We explained that the hostess, who was standing at the bar looking at her phone, was supposed to be checking if we could be seated.  He walked over to her and "asked" but came back very quickly and reiterated that they couldn't seat us without a reservation. While he was checking, we whipped out the phone and found MULTIPLE reservation periods available as soon as 30 minutes in the future (minimum amount of time that Open Table will show).  30 minutes later, we were seated WITH our reservation.

<UserId.>113669553636359461479< /UserId.><review>I went here two times for lunch. The first time I had their house special chicken. The second time I tried the garlic beef with pad thai noodles, which came with an appetizer egg drop-like soup. Overall, the food is nothing spectacular. Like Talesai in Studio City, Anajak Thai's food is pretty Americanized, thus it's not really authentic tasting like Krua Thai, Sanumluang and Hollywood Thai. At times, the food even has that sense of a typical Americanized Chinese restaurant taste and vibe. Their house special chicken was pretty good, although their pad thai was a bit bland, their garlic beef was okay, and their soup a bit on the bland side as well.

In conclusion, this is an edible place to eat if you're in the area looking for a quick lunch bite. But don't drive out of your way to come here. There are so many other better Thai restaurants in LA. Unfortunately, Ventura Boulevard doesn't have too many great Thai restaurants.</review></record></dataset><record>

<Text>This is the BEST Thai food, I have ever eaten! The owner and his wife are gems, and this place has become a special treat for my husband, Dan, and I. We love the following dishes the BEST:
1) To start the Potstickers and the Shrimp Supreme are favs! That special sauce that is prepared for the Shrimp Supreme, is amazing!
2) Entrees, the Anajak Thai Chicken gives you an amazing combination of cashews with chilis and you can ask for only white meat (fore a mere $2 extra), worth it if you like chicken breast.
The Panang Curry with Shrimp and Roti, is just amazing. Chef Ricky really know the balance between the sauce shrimp, and dipping the roti into the sauce is a treat.
Dan loves the Summer Noodles, and the Lad Na, and alternates between the two every time we go. Both are mouth-watering, and sometimes, we opt for the Summer Noodles, or the Pad Thai, really, they are all amazing.
3) Dessert - Lychee fruit with pineapple. Very light, cleanses the palate, and sets you up for the rest of the night.

< review>
It takes a lot for me to leave a 1 star review on a business, but I feel it is warranted in this case. Jamba Juice advertises fresh pressed juice and charges an arm and a leg for it. Understandable, as pressed juice requires a lot of material to produce even a 16oz cups worth. I paid almost $8 for 16oz. The girl began by pressing some apples, good start... but then to that added scoops of what appeared to be canned, crushed pineapple and a small handful of spinach to it and then blended it... like in a blender. It was served to me like that, and I only got about 3 sips out of it before it all turned to thick pulp i couldn't get through the straw. I can go to Blender in the Grass and pay less for actual pressed juice. I don't know if this is common practice for all Jamba Juice locations, but it's false advertising and shows that this is a company that doesn't really care about quality as long as they save a few bucks.< /review>

Unfortunetly, I couldn't get off work early enough to go with her but would pick her up after. My mother had the appointment scheduled at 7pm & arrived at 630pm. From our previous experience they denied to see her because she was a couple of minutes late so she made sure she got there 30 minutes early. They did not assist her until 730pm. Which I thought was unfair since the previous time she was only 15 mins late & they denied to see her. Nonetheless she got seen by the doctor & was charged another doctor's visit only for the doctor to read the results of the blood test off a piece of paper. Which I thought was completely unfair, I could've easily just asked for her records & had my doctor read it or research what it was. But anyways after they read her results they tell her she needs 3 shots. One of them being for the flu. I was so upset when I found out they told her to get one & pay for it when flu season is over. On top of that she got extremely sick the next day with the flu. So she basically paid just to get sick. But my biggest complaint is probably the three receptionists behind the counter. I arrived at 730pm and waited for my mother until 830pm. I was sitting with another gentlemen in the lobby waiting for my mother & he was waiting for a family member. One of the receptionists comes in & asks us are we waiting for someone. We both responded "yes". 30 minutes pass & I am now the only one waiting in the lobby. The 1st receptionists is sitting at the front desk on a computer & then another one comes in. She talks to the girl on the computer and I hear them talking about me. Then she asks me the question again, "are you waiting for someone?" I look at the receptionist on the computer in the eyes & say, "yes, she already asked me that." Then they look at each other & both sit down. One of them leaves & comes back with I believe the supervisor & she looks at me & asks me again, "hi are you waiting for someone? Do you want to go inside & sit with your mom?" At this point I am annoyed & realize that it is their closing time but don't understand why they keep pressing me when I told them at least twice that I am waiting for someone. So I responded in a very sassy manner, "yes I already told all of you I am waiting for someone and is there a problem with me sitting here? Like what's the problem? Can i not sit here?" They all looked shocked & said, "oh no no it's fine." Then sit down & start whispering amongst themselves. At this point I am getting irritated because they're making such a big deal about me sitting in the lobby. I couldn't hear what they were saying but it was making me very uncomfortable. Finally my mother comes out & I hear her bickering with the supervisor saying that the supervisor was attempting to write her a referral for an exam that the doctor never recommended. I could hear them from the other side of the lobby & she spent at least 15 minutes trying to give her this referral when she didn't need. My mother kept telling her that it's not what the doctor said but she refused to listen & said since the doctor left that she would call her back to let her know. Till this day we have still not received any communication about what the doctor said. My mom instead of arguing with her left with me & we could hear them laughing as we were leaving. I am never taking my mother to this establishment again & I advise that if you do come here please be assertive & ask a lot of questions. Off of this interaction I could tell there was no communication between the doctors & his nurses/receptionists. Medical visits are expensive & for the doctor to say she doesn't need it but then the nurse/receptionists to say she does, is confusing & can be a waste of money. Not only that but the service here was trash, why were they so concerned with me sitting in the lobby? <user>110452130512160064881<//user><Name>Sabrina Gomez</Name>< Date>
1535558987161< /Date>
<rate>2< /rate>< review>
It was my son's first visit.  I was a bit disappointed with some of the staff on how "routinely" his experience was.  I was hoping a child's first visit would have been a bit more special.  The check up was in a large room which was filled with 2 big islands that hold computers (in which case I was not able to see my son's x-rays), and with about 6 dental chairs.  The room was chaotic filled with patients, parents, dental assistants, and dentists.  It was a lot of traffic.  Again, being a first visit I would have hoped for a private room, an option to see my son's x-rays up close, and just a less noisier room.  Now comes the part were I was alarmed.  I paid my $52 copayment, PPO insurance, which I was told included the exam, x-rays, and cleaning.  At the end of the visit I was told my son, may or may not, need two baby root canals and 2 or maybe 3 silver caps on his molars.  Which sounds a bit strange since he is not experiencing any pain, and with that degree of work, I would think he would have problems eating, or bigger problems that would have been brought to our attention.  After reviewing the total costs, I was told I had a balance due from today's visit due to x-rays.  I am now alarmed with the billing at Children's Dental FunZone.  I was told my copayment included the x-rays.  When I questioned why there were additional fees, I was told sometimes Dentist request additional x-rays to get a better view.  In this case, in my son's case, this was not accurate.  My son's x-rays were taken PRIOR to seeing the dentist, and was never asked to retake any. Our visit was simple, pay copayment, x-rays taken, dental exam with dentist.  We did not have two visits to the x-ray room.  At this point, I'm not sure if I feel confident with how they will try to bill us for any other procedures or if any future exams.  The fancy aquarium, theatre room, and free toy didn't impress with the possible extra fees.</review>

<user_id>113334337420093390424< /user_id><Name>Jacquelyn Evans</Name><Time>1250195181977</Time><rating>5</rating>< review>
Before coming here i took my 5yo and 2yo to the dental playground in covina and they had a traumatizing experience. it was screaming and crying for help the entire time so i wanted to at lest try and find a more compassionate and friendly dentist. after coming here i found exactly what i was looking for. the waiting area put my kids in wonderful moods. there was a huge aquarium, balloons everywhere, video games, disney movies playing, i was shocked. when it was time to get x-rays and see the dentist both of my kids were so laid back and happy that they didnt care that they had to open their mouths, close them, hold still. they just obeyed without a word of protest. my daughter needed work done and i found the dentist to be warm and friendly. she discussed all my options and told me to call back when i made a decision and they could arrange an appointment from there. she didnt pressure me into making decisions. when it came time to have the work done the dentist and assistant talked to my daughter the entire time to try and put her at ease, and they did the best job i couldve ever hoped for. i highly recommend this place and my children will be going here from now on.</review>
